  <script type="text/javascript" data-do-not-move="true">
        //<![CDATA[
        var AmbientContext = null;

        (function(){
            var root = (function(){return this;}).call(null);

            var GetCookie = function(name){
                var cookies = root.document.cookie ? root.document.cookie.split('; ') : [];
                for (var i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {
                    var pos = cookies[i].indexOf('=');
                    if (name === root.decodeURIComponent(cookies[i].slice(0, pos)))
                    {
                        var cookie = cookies[i].slice(pos + 1).replace(/\+/g, ' ');
                        cookie = root.decodeURIComponent(cookie);
                        return cookie;
                    }
                }
            };

            var JsonDeserialize = function(content) {
                return root.JSON && root.JSON.parse ? root.JSON.parse(content) : (new Function('return (' + content + ')'))();
            };

            try {
                AmbientContext = GetCookie('AmbientContext');
                AmbientContext = AmbientContext && JsonDeserialize(AmbientContext);
            } catch(ex) {
            } finally {
                AmbientContext = AmbientContext || null;
            }
        })();
        //]]>
    </script>

     <div class="topic" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml"> 
      <h1 class="title">Authentication Functions</h1> 
      <!--Content type: HTML. Transform: webcollection2mtps.xslt.--> 
      <div id="mainSection"> 
       <div class="clsServerSDKContent"> 
       </div> 
       <p>Authentication functions are categorized according to usage as follows:</p> 
       <p> </p>
       <ul> 
        <li><a href="#sspi_functions">SSPI Functions</a>
         <ul> 
          <li><a href="#package_management">Package Management</a></li> 
          <li><a href="#credential_management">Credential Management</a></li>

          <li><a href="#message_support">Message Support</a></li> 
         </ul> </li>

        <li><a href="#functions_implemented_by_user_mode_ssp_aps">Functions Implemented by User-mode SSP/APs</a></li> 
        <li><a href="#lsa_functions_called_by_ssp_aps">LSA Functions Called by SSP/APs</a></li> 
        <li><a href="#lsa_functions_called_by_user_mode_ssp_aps">LSA Functions Called By User-mode SSP/APs</a></li> 
        <li><a href="#gina_export_functions">GINA Export Functions</a></li> 
        <li><a href="#logon_functions">Logon User Functions</a></li> 
        <li><a href="#winlogon_support_functions">Winlogon Support Functions</a></li> 
        <li><a href="#network_provider_functions">Network Provider Functions</a>
         <ul> 
          <li><a href="#network_provider_functions_sub">Functions Implemented by Network Providers</a></li> 
          <li><a href="#support_functions">Support Functions</a></li> 
          <li><a href="#connection_notification_functions">Connection Notification Functions</a></li> 
         </ul> </li> 
        <li><a href="#lsa_logon_functions">LSA Logon Functions</a></li> 
        <li><a href="#functions_implemented_by_authentication_packages">Functions Implemented by Authentication Packages</a></li>

       <h2><a id="sspi_functions">
         <!----></a><a id="SSPI_FUNCTIONS">
         <!----></a>SSPI Functions</h2> 
       <p>Security Support Provider Interface (SSPI) functions fall into the following major categories.</p> 
       <ul> 
        <li><a href="#package_management">Package management</a><p>Functions that list the available <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security packages</em></a> and select a package.</p> </li> 
        <li><a href="#credential_management">Credential management</a><p>Functions that create and work with handles to the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721572(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_credentials_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">credentials</em></a> of <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721603(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_principal_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">principals</em></a>.</p> </li> 
        <li><a href="#context_management">Context management</a><p>Functions that use credentials handles to create a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_context_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security context</em></a>.</p> </li> 
        <li><a href="#message_support">Message support</a><p>Functions that use security contexts to ensure message <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721588(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_integrity_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">integrity</em></a> and <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721603(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_privacy_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">privacy</em></a> during message exchanges over the secured connection. Integrity is achieved through message signing and signature verification. Privacy is achieved through message encryption and decryption.</p> </li> 
       </ul> 
       <h3><a id="package_management">
         <!----></a><a id="PACKAGE_MANAGEMENT">
         <!----></a>Package Management</h3> 
       <p>SSPI package management functions initiate a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security package</em></a>, enumerate available packages, and query the attributes of a security package. The following SSPI functions provide management services for security packages.</p> 
       <table responsive="true" summary="table"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr responsive="true">
          <th scope="col">Function</th>
          <th scope="col">Description</th>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375397(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">EnumerateSecurityPackages</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Lists available security packages and their capabilities.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa376103(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">InitSecurityInterface</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Retrieves a pointer to a security support provider (SSP) dispatch table.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa379359(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">QuerySecurityPackageInfo</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Retrieves information about a specified <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security package</em></a>. This information includes the bounds on sizes of authentication information, <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721572(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_credentials_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">credentials</em></a>, and contexts.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
        </tbody>
       </table> 
       <p>&nbsp;</p> 
       <h3><a id="credential_management">
         <!----></a><a id="CREDENTIAL_MANAGEMENT">
         <!----></a>Credential Management</h3> 
       <p>SSPI credential management functions provide a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721572(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_credentials_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">credentials</em></a> handle, a reference to an opaque security object, for accessing a principal. The security object is opaque because the application has access only to the handle and not to the actual contents of the structure.</p> 
       <p>All references to the contents of a credential context are through the object's handle and the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security package</em></a> dereferences the handle to access the specifics of credentials. A credential handle is a 64-bit value between {0x00000000, 0x00000000} and {0xFFFFFFFF, 0xFFFFFFFE}.</p> 
       <p>Applications use the credentials handle with <a href="#context_management">context management</a> functions to create a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_context_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security context</em></a>.</p> 
       <p>Credential management functions also release credential handles and query the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721532(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_attribute_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">attributes</em></a> of <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721572(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_credentials_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">credentials</em></a>. At present, the name associated with a credential is the only attribute that can be queried.</p> 
       <p>The following functions are used with credentials management.</p> 
       <table responsive="true" summary="table"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr responsive="true">
          <th scope="col">Function</th>
          <th scope="col">Description</th>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374712(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">AcquireCredentialsHandle (General)</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Acquires a handle to the preexisting credentials of a specified principal.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375409(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">ExportSecurityContext</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Exports a security context into a context buffer.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375417(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">FreeCredentialsHandle</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Releases a credential handle and associated resources.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375502(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">ImportSecurityContext</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Imports a security context exported by using <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375409(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">ExportSecurityContext</strong></a> into the current process.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa379342(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">QueryCredentialsAttributes</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Retrieves the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721532(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_attribute_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">attributes</em></a> of a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721572(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_credentials_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">credential</em></a>, such as the name associated with the credential.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
        </tbody>
       </table> 
       <p>&nbsp;</p> 
       <h3><a id="context_management">
         <!----></a><a id="CONTEXT_MANAGEMENT">
         <!----></a>Context Management</h3> 
       <p>SSPI context management functions create and use <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_context_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security contexts</em></a>.</p> 
       <p>In a communication link, the client and server cooperate to create a shared security context. The client and server both use the security context with <a href="#message_support">message support</a> functions to ensure message <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721588(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_integrity_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">integrity</em></a> and <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721603(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_privacy_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">privacy</em></a> during the connection.</p> 
       <p>Security contexts are opaque security objects. Information in the security context is not available to the application. Context management functions create and use context handles and the security package dereferences the context handle to access its security content.</p> 
       <p>A context handle is a 64-bit value between {0x00000000, 0x00000000} and {0xFFFFFFFF, 0xFFFFFFFE}.</p> 
       <p>The following functions are used with context management.</p> 
       <table responsive="true" summary="table"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr responsive="true">
          <th scope="col">Function</th>
          <th scope="col">Description</th>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374703(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">AcceptSecurityContext (General)</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Used by a server to create a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_context_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security context</em></a> based on an opaque message received from a client.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374724(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">ApplyControlToken</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Applies a supplemental security message to an existing security context.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374764(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">CompleteAuthToken</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Completes an authentication token. This function is used by protocols, such as DCE, that need to revise the security information after the transport application has updated some message parameters.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375354(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">DeleteSecurityContext</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Frees a security context and associated resources.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375416(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">FreeContextBuffer</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Frees a memory buffer allocated by a security package.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375497(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">ImpersonateSecurityContext</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Impersonates the security context to appear as the client to the system.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375506(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">InitializeSecurityContext (General)</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Used by a client to initiate a security context by generating an opaque message to be passed to a server.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa379326(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">QueryContextAttributes (General)</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Enables a transport application to query a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security package</em></a> for certain <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721532(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_attribute_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">attributes</em></a> of a security <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721572(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_context_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">context</em></a>.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa379355(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">QuerySecurityContextToken</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Obtains the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721532(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_access_token_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">access token</em></a> for a client <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_context_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security context</em></a> and uses it directly.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380137(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SetContextAttributes</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Enables a transport application to set <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721532(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_attribute_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">attributes</em></a> of a security <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721572(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_context_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">context</em></a> for a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security package</em></a>. This function is supported only by the Schannel security package.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa379446(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">RevertSecurityContext</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Allows a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security package</em></a> to discontinue the impersonation of the caller and restore its own <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_context_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security context</em></a>.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
        </tbody>
       </table> 
       <p>&nbsp;</p> 
       <h3><a id="message_support">
         <!----></a><a id="MESSAGE_SUPPORT">
         <!----></a>Message Support</h3> 
       <p>SSPI message support functions enable an application to transmit and receive tamper-resistant messages and to encrypt and decrypt messages. These functions work with one or more buffers that contain a message and with a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_context_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security context</em></a> created by the <a href="#context_management">context management</a> functions. The functions' behavior differs based on whether a connection, <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721573(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_datagram_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">datagram</em></a>, or stream context is in use. For a description of these differences, see <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380494(v=vs.85).aspx">SSPI Context Semantics</a>.</p> 
       <p>The following functions provide security support for messages.</p> 
       <table responsive="true" summary="table"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr responsive="true">
          <th scope="col">Function</th>
          <th scope="col">Description</th>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375211(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">DecryptMessage (General)</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Decrypts an encrypted message by using the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_session_key_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">session key</em></a> from a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_context_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security context</em></a>.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375378(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">EncryptMessage (General)</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Encrypts a message by using the session key from a security context.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378736(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">MakeSignature</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Generates a cryptographic checksum of the message, and also includes sequencing information to prevent message loss or insertion.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380540(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">VerifySignature</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Verifies the signature of a message received that was signed by the sender by using the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378736(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">MakeSignature</strong></a> function.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
        </tbody>
       </table> 
       <p>&nbsp;</p> 
       <h2><a id="functions_implemented_by_ssp_aps">
         <!----></a><a id="FUNCTIONS_IMPLEMENTED_BY_SSP_APS">
         <!----></a>Functions Implemented by SSP/APs</h2> 
       <p>The following functions are implemented by <a href="#sspi_functions">security packages</a> contained in <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_support_provider_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Security Support Provider</em></a>/<a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721532(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_authentication_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Authentication Packages</em></a> (SSP/APs).</p> 
       <p>In the following tables, the first set of functions is implemented by Windows&nbsp;XP SSP/AP security packages. The second set of functions is implemented by SSP/AP security packages only.</p> 
       <p>The <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721592(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_local_security_authority_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Local Security Authority</em></a> (LSA) accesses these functions by using the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380114(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SECPKG_FUNCTION_TABLE</strong></a> structure provided by the SSP/AP's <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380175(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SpLsaModeInitialize</strong></a> function.</p> 
       <p>The following functions are implemented by all authentication packages.</p>

       <p>&nbsp;</p> 
       <h2><a id="functions_implemented_by_user_mode_ssp_aps">
         <!----></a><a id="FUNCTIONS_IMPLEMENTED_BY_USER_MODE_SSP_APS">
         <!----></a>Functions Implemented by User-mode SSP/APs</h2> 
       <p>The following functions are implemented by <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_support_provider_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security support provider</em></a>/<a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721532(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_authentication_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">authentication packages</em></a> (SSP/APs) that can be loaded into client/server applications.</p> 
       <p>An SSP/AP indicates that it implements the user-mode functions by returning <strong>TRUE</strong> in the <em>MappedContext</em> parameter of the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380172(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SpInitLsaModeContext</strong></a> and <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380154(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SpAcceptLsaModeContext</strong></a> functions. The <strong>SpInitLsaModeContext</strong> function is used by the client side of a transport level application, while <strong>SpAcceptLsaModeContext</strong> is used by the server side.</p> 
       <p>Loading an SSP/AP into the client process or server process is handled by the security provider DLL, either Security.dll or Secur32.dll. The security provider DLL loads the SSP/AP by locating the address of the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380185(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SpUserModeInitialize</strong></a> function implemented by the SSP/AP and calling it. This function returns a set of tables that contain pointers to the user-mode functions implemented in each <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security package</em></a>.</p> 
       <p>After the SSP/AP is loaded into the client or server process, the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721592(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_local_security_authority_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Local Security Authority</em></a> (LSA) will copy the security context information (returned by <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380172(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SpInitLsaModeContext</strong></a> or <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380154(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SpAcceptLsaModeContext</strong></a>) and any additional context-related data to the process and call the security package's <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380173(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SpInitUserModeContext</strong></a> function.</p> 
       <p>Client/server applications access user-mode functionality by calling <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380493(v=vs.85).aspx">Security Support Provider Interface</a> (SSPI) functions. The SSPI functions are mapped by the security provider DLL by using the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380122(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SECPKG_USER_FUNCTION_TABLE</strong></a> supplied by the package.</p> 
       <table responsive="true" summary="table"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr responsive="true">
          <th scope="col">Function</th>
          <th scope="col">Description</th>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380158(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SpCompleteAuthToken</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Completes an authentication token. </p> <p>Implements the SSPI <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374764(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">CompleteAuthToken</strong></a> function.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>

       <h2><a id="lsa_functions_called_by_ssp_aps">
         <!----></a><a id="LSA_FUNCTIONS_CALLED_BY_SSP_APS">
         <!----></a>LSA Functions Called by SSP/APs</h2> 
       <p>The <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721592(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_local_security_authority_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Local Security Authority</em></a> (LSA) provides the following functions to <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security packages</em></a> deployed in <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_support_provider_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security support provider</em></a>/<a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721532(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_authentication_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">authentication packages</em></a> (SSP/APs). The functions are available in the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380114(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LSA_SECPKG_FUNCTION_TABLE</strong></a> structure and can be called while the SSP/AP is loaded into the LSA's process space. The following functions are available to all APs.</p> 
       <table responsive="true" summary="table"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr responsive="true">
          <th scope="col">Function</th>
          <th scope="col">Description</th>
         </tr>

          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Adds user <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721572(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_credentials_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">credentials</em></a>.</p> </td>
         </tr>

          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Allocates memory in the address space of the package's client.</p> </td>
         </tr>

          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Called by <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security packages</em></a> to impersonate the package user.</p> </td>

         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378741(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">MapBuffer</strong></a> </td>

          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Provides a mechanism whereby the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security package</em></a> is notified. Notification can occur at fixed intervals, when an event object is signaled, or during certain system events.</p> </td>

       <h2><a id="lsa_functions_called_by_user_mode_ssp_aps">

       <p>A <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security package</em></a> in a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_support_provider_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security support provider</em></a>/<a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721532(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_authentication_package_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">authentication package</em></a> (SSP/AP) executing in a user-mode process can use the pointers in the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380108(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SECPKG_DLL_FUNCTIONS</strong></a> table to access the following functions.</p>

          <td data-th="PSDK status"> <p>Frees memory that was previously allocated by using <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374721(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">AllocateHeap</strong></a>.</p> </td>

This is the first call made by <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721635(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_winlogon_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Winlogon</em></a> to the GINA DLL. <strong>WlxNegotiate</strong> allows the GINA to verify that it supports the installed version of Winlogon.</p> </td>

          <td data-th="Description"> <p><a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721635(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_winlogon_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Winlogon</em></a> calls this function to collect valid authentication and identification information.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>

         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380583(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">WlxScreenSaverNotify</strong></a> </td>

         </tr>

         </tr>

          <td data-th="Description"> <p><a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721635(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_winlogon_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Winlogon</em></a> calls this function when it receives a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_secure_attention_sequence_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">secure attention sequence</em></a> (SAS) and the workstation is locked.</p> </td>

          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Attempts to log a user on to the local computer.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378189(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LogonUserEx</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Attempts to log a user on to the local computer. This function is an extended version of the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378184(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LogonUser</strong></a> function and retrieves information about the logged-on user's <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_identifier_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security identifier</em></a> (SID), profile, and quota limits.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/bb540756(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LogonUserExExW</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>The <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/bb540756(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LogonUserExExW</strong></a> function attempts to log a user on to the local computer. This function is not declared in a public header and has no associated import library. You must use the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms684175(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LoadLibrary</strong></a> and <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms683212(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">GetProcAddress</strong></a> functions to dynamically link to Advapi32.dll.</p> </td>
         </tr>

       <h2><a id="winlogon_support_functions">
         <!----></a><a id="WINLOGON_SUPPORT_FUNCTIONS">
         <!----></a>Winlogon Support Functions</h2> 
       <p><a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721584(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_gina_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">GINA</em></a> DLLs can call the following <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721635(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_winlogon_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Winlogon</em></a> support functions.</p> 
       <div class="alert">
        <strong>Note</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp; GINA DLLs are ignored in Windows&nbsp;Vista.
       </div> 
       <div>
        &nbsp;
       </div> 
       <table responsive="true" summary="table"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr responsive="true">
          <th scope="col">Function</th>
          <th scope="col">Called by GINA</th>

       <p>The following topics provide reference information for the network provider functions.</p>

          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Retrieves the names of buttons to add to a property dialog box for a network resource.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378800(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">NPGetResourceInformation</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Separates the part of a network resource accessed through the WNet API from the part accessed through APIs specific to the resource type.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378801(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">NPGetResourceParent</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Retrieves the parent of a specified network resource in the browse hierarchy.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378802(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">NPGetUniversalName</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Retrieves the universal name of a network resource. The <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378802(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">NPGetUniversalName</strong></a> function can retrieve this universal name in UNC format or in the older, remote-name format.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378803(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">NPGetUser</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Retrieves the value of the current default user name or the user name used to establish a network connection.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378805(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">NPOpenEnum</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Opens an enumeration of network resources or existing connections. The <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378805(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">NPOpenEnum</strong></a> function must be called to obtain a valid handle for an enumeration.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378807(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">NPPropertyDialog</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Called when the user clicks a button added by using the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378807(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">NPPropertyDialog</strong></a> function. The <strong>NPPropertyDialog</strong> function is called only for file and directory network properties.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378808(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">NPSearchDialog</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Enables network vendors to supply their own form of browsing and search, beyond the hierarchical view presented in the <strong>Connection</strong> dialog box.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
        </tbody>
       </table>

       <h3><a id="support_functions">
         <!----></a><a id="SUPPORT_FUNCTIONS">
         <!----></a>Support Functions</h3> 
       <p>The following function is implemented by the operating system and can be called by network providers.</p> 
       <table responsive="true" summary="table"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr responsive="true">
          <th scope="col">Function</th>
          <th scope="col">Description</th>
         </tr>

          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Sets extended error information. Network providers should call this function instead of <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms680627(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SetLastError</strong></a>.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
        </tbody>
       </table>

       <h3><a id="connection_notification_functions">
         <!----></a><a id="CONNECTION_NOTIFICATION_FUNCTIONS">
         <!----></a>Connection Notification Functions</h3> 
       <p>The following functions are implemented by applications that need to receive notification from the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721594(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_multiple_provider_router_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Multiple Provider Router</em></a> (MPR) when a network resource is connected or disconnected. For more information about how to write an application that receives such notifications, see <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa379365(v=vs.85).aspx">Receiving Connection Notifications</a>.</p> 
       <table responsive="true" summary="table"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr responsive="true">
          <th scope="col">Function</th>
          <th scope="col">Description</th>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374717(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">AddConnectNotify</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Called before and after each add connection operation (<a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa385410(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">WNetAddConnection</strong></a>, <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa385413(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">WNetAddConnection2</strong></a>, and <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa385418(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">WNetAddConnection3</strong></a>).</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374749(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">CancelConnectNotify</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Called before and after each cancel connection operation (<a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa385423(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">WNetCancelConnection</strong></a> or <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa385427(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">WNetCancelConnection2</strong></a>).</p> </td>
         </tr> 
        </tbody>
       </table>

       <h2><a id="lsa_logon_functions">
         <!----></a><a id="LSA_LOGON_FUNCTIONS">
         <!----></a>LSA Logon Functions</h2> 
       <p>The following <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721592(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_local_security_authority_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Local Security Authority</em></a> (LSA) authentication functions authenticate and log on users, and they provide logon session information.</p> 
       <table responsive="true" summary="table"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr responsive="true">
          <th scope="col">Function</th>
          <th scope="col">Description</th>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378261(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaCallAuthenticationPackage</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Requests a package-specific service from an authentication package.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378265(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaConnectUntrusted</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Establishes an untrusted connection to the LSA.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378269(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaDeregisterLogonProcess</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Disconnects from the LSA and frees resources allocated to the caller's context.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378275(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaEnumerateLogonSessions</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Retrieves <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721592(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_locally_unique_identifier_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">locally unique identifiers</em></a> (LUIDs) for existing logon sessions.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378279(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaFreeReturnBuffer</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Frees memory allocated for a buffer returned to a caller.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378290(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaGetLogonSessionData</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Retrieves information about a specified logon session.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378292(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaLogonUser</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Authenticates user logon data against stored credentials. If successful, it creates a new logon session and returns a user token.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378297(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaLookupAuthenticationPackage</strong></a> </td>

         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378303(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaQueryDomainInformationPolicy</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Retrieves domain information from the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721912(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Policy</strong></a> object.</p> </td>
         </tr>

          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Retrieves forest trust information for the specified <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721592(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_local_security_authority_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Local Security Authority</em></a>&nbsp;<a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms722464(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">TrustedDomain</strong></a> object.</p> </td>
         </tr>

          <td data-th="Description"> <p>sets the forest trust information for a specified <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721592(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_local_security_authority_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Local Security Authority</em></a>&nbsp;<a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms722464(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">TrustedDomain</strong></a> object.</p> </td>

       <h2><a id="functions_implemented_by_authentication_packages">
         <!----></a><a id="FUNCTIONS_IMPLEMENTED_BY_AUTHENTICATION_PACKAGES">
         <!----></a>Functions Implemented by Authentication Packages</h2> 
       <p>Custom authentication packages must implement these functions, which are called by the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721592(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_local_security_authority_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Local Security Authority</em></a> (LSA). These functions are implemented by the MSV1_0 and Kerberos authentication packages provided by Microsoft.</p> 
       <table responsive="true" summary="table"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr responsive="true">
          <th scope="col">Function</th>
          <th scope="col">Description</th>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378194(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApCallPackage</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Called when the authentication package's identifier has been specified in a call to <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378261(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaCallAuthenticationPackage</strong></a> by an application that is using a trusted connection.</p> <p>This function provides a way for logon applications to communicate directly with authentication packages.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378212(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApCallPackagePassthrough</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Called when the authentication package's identifier has been specified in a call to <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378261(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaCallAuthenticationPackage</strong></a> for a pass-through logon request.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378218(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApCallPackageUntrusted</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Called when the authentication package's identifier has been specified in a call to <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378261(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaCallAuthenticationPackage</strong></a> by an application using an untrusted connection. This function is used for communicating with processes that do not have the SeTcbPrivilege privilege.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378233(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApInitializePackage</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Called during system initialization to permit the authentication package to perform initialization tasks.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378238(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApLogonTerminated</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Called when a logon session ends to permit the authentication package to free any resources allocated for the logon session.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378244(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApLogonUser</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Called when the authentication package has been specified in a call to <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378292(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaLogonUser</strong></a>. This function authenticates a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_principal_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security principal's</em></a> logon data.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378248(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApLogonUserEx</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Identical to <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378244(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApLogonUser</strong></a> except that it returns the workstation name for audit purposes.</p> <p>An authentication package can implement <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378244(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApLogonUser</strong></a>, <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378248(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApLogonUserEx</strong></a>, or <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378257(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApLogonUserEx2</strong></a>. It does not need to implement them all.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378257(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApLogonUserEx2</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Identical to <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378248(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApLogonUserEx</strong></a> except that it returns the security principal's primary and supplemental credentials. An authentication package can implement <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378244(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApLogonUser</strong></a>, <strong>LsaApLogonUserEx</strong>, or <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378257(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApLogonUserEx2</strong></a>. It does not need to implement them all.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
        </tbody>
       </table> 
       <p>&nbsp;</p> 
       <h2><a id="lsa_functions_called_by_authentication_packages">
         <!----></a><a id="LSA_FUNCTIONS_CALLED_BY_AUTHENTICATION_PACKAGES">
         <!----></a>LSA Functions Called by Authentication Packages</h2> 
       <p>The following <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721592(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_local_security_authority_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Local Security Authority</em></a> (LSA) functions can be called from a custom authentication package. When the LSA calls <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa378233(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">LsaApInitializePackage</strong></a> to initialize the package, it passes a table of support functions.</p> 
       <table responsive="true" summary="table"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr responsive="true">
          <th scope="col">Function</th>
          <th scope="col">Description</th>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374718(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">AddCredential</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Adds credentials to a logon session.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374720(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">AllocateClientBuffer</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Allocates a buffer in the client's address space.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374722(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">AllocateLsaHeap</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Allocates buffers that must be returned from the authentication package to the LSA.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374772(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">CopyFromClientBuffer</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Copies the contents of a buffer in the client's address space into a local buffer.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374774(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">CopyToClientBuffer</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Copies the contents of a local buffer into the client's address space.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374776(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">CreateLogonSession</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Used by authentication packages to create a logon session.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375350(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">DeleteCredential</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Deletes an existing credential.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375352(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">DeleteLogonSession</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Cleans up any logon sessions created while determining whether a user's authentication information is legitimate.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>

       <h2><a id="sasl_functions">
         <!----></a><a id="SASL_FUNCTIONS">
         <!----></a>SASL Functions</h2> 
       <p>The Simple Authentication and Security Layer (SASL) provides the following functions.</p> 
       <table responsive="true" summary="table"> 
        <tbody>
         <tr responsive="true">
          <th scope="col">Functions</th>
          <th scope="col">Description</th>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Functions"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa379453(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SaslAcceptSecurityContext</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description">Wraps a standard call to the SSPI <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374703(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">AcceptSecurityContext (General)</strong></a> function and includes creation of SASL server cookies.</td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Functions"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa379455(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SaslEnumerateProfiles</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description">Lists the packages that provide a SASL interface.</td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Functions"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa379456(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SaslGetContextOption</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description">Retrieves the specified property of the specified SASL context.</td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Functions"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa379459(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SaslGetProfilePackage</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description">Returns the package information for the specified package.</td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Functions"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa379461(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SaslIdentifyPackage</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description">Returns the negotiate prefix that matches the specified SASL negotiation buffer.</td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Functions"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa379463(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SaslInitializeSecurityContext</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description">Wraps a standard call to the SSPI <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375506(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">InitializeSecurityContext (General)</strong></a> function and processes SASL server cookies from the server.</td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Functions"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa379464(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SaslSetContextOption</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description">Sets the value of the specified property for the specified SASL context.</td>
         </tr> 
        </tbody>
       </table>

          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401700(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiDecryptAuthIdentity</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Decrypts the specified encrypted credential.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401701(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiEncodeAuthIdentityAsStrings</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Encodes the specified authentication identity as three strings.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401702(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiEncodeStringsAsAuthIdentity</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Encodes a set of three credential strings as an authentication identity structure.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401703(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiEncryptAuthIdentity</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Encrypts the specified identity structure.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401704(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiExcludePackage</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Creates a new identity structure that is a copy of the specified identity structure modified to exclude the specified <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_support_provider_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">security support provider</em></a> (SSP).</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401705(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiFreeAuthIdentity</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Frees the memory allocated for the specified identity structure.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401706(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiGetCredUIContext</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Retrieves context information from a credential provider.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401707(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiGetTargetHostName</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Gets the host name associated with the specified target.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401708(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiIsAuthIdentityEncrypted</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Indicates whether the specified identity structure is encrypted.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401709(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiIsPromptingNeeded</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Indicates whether an error returned after a call to either the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375506(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">InitializeSecurityContext</strong></a> or the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa374703(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">AcceptSecurityContext</strong></a> function requires an additional call to the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401714(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiPromptForCredentials</strong></a> function.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401710(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiLocalFree</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Frees the memory associated with the specified buffer.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401711(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiMarshalAuthIdentity</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Serializes the specified identity structure into a byte array.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401712(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiPrepareForCredRead</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Generates a target name and credential type from the specified identity structure.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401713(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiPrepareForCredWrite</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Generates values from an identity structure that can be passed as the values of parameters in a call to the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa375187(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">CredWrite</strong></a> function.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401714(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiPromptForCredentials</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Allows a <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721625(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_security_support_provider_interface_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">Security Support Provider Interface </em></a>(SSPI) application to prompt a user to enter credentials.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401715(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiUnmarshalAuthIdentity</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Deserializes the specified array of byte values into an identity structure.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401716(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiUnmarshalCredUIContext</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Deserializes credential information obtained by a credential provider during a previous call to the <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/bb776043(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">ICredentialProvider::SetSerialization</strong></a> method.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401717(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiUpdateCredentials</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Updates the credentials associated with the specified context.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401718(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiValidateAuthIdentity</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Indicates whether the specified identity structure is valid.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/dd401719(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">SspiZeroAuthIdentity</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Fills the block of memory associated with the specified identity structure with zeros.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
         <tr>
          <td data-th="Function"> <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/aa380580(v=vs.85).aspx"><strong xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">WlxQueryTsLogonCredentials</strong></a> </td>
          <td data-th="Description"> <p>Called by a replacement <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721584(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_gina_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">GINA</em></a> DLL to retrieve <a href="https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windows/desktop/ms721572(v=vs.85).aspx#_security_credentials_gly"><em xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml">credentials</em></a> information if Terminal Services is enabled. The GINA DLL can then use this information to fill in a logon box automatically and attempt to log the user in.</p> </td>
         </tr> 
        </tbody>
       </table> 
       <p>&nbsp;</p> 
       <p>&nbsp;</p>
